Foreign Important Telegrams

Unprecedented Gathering in Geneva Today

Political Leaders from Various Countries Assemble

To Discuss Important World Issues

MacDonald Arrives in Geneva with Tardieu

Geneva Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 20th: This Friday will see an unprecedented gathering of politicians from various countries, discussing the most complex issues since the Paris Peace Conference. All major powers, except Japan, are sending their prime ministers or foreign ministers. Many smaller countries are also sending their foreign ministers. The issues under consideration include Franco-German rapprochement, the Franco-Italian naval agreement, arms reduction, the economic and financial crisis in the Danube region, disputes in the Far East, and reparations and war debts—all major world events.

Paris Dispatch from Reuters on the 20th: The French elections are about to begin, but French Premier Tardieu has decided to travel to Geneva with British Prime Minister MacDonald today, which has surprised many. It shows that Tardieu is deeply aware of the importance of being in Geneva at the same time as the prime ministers of Britain, America, and Germany. The British and French prime ministers held a closed-door meeting for forty minutes. Although no official statement was issued, Tardieu said that they discussed various matters, especially focusing on Geneva. From this, it is clear that their discussions mostly concerned the issue of arms reduction. Tardieu did not express pessimism about arms reduction. British Prime Minister MacDonald arrived here by plane at 5:40 PM. After resting briefly at the British Embassy, he went to the French Foreign Ministry. In the evening, he boarded a train to Geneva with the French Premier. When the British Prime Minister left London, it was raining heavily, but he decided to travel by plane, saying that flying in the rain was the most pleasant form of travel. The British Prime Minister's eye ailment has not fully recovered, and his doctor is also traveling to Geneva tonight.

Geneva Dispatch from Havas on the 21st: French Premier Tardieu and British Prime Minister MacDonald arrived here at 8:00 AM this morning. Tardieu is expected to stay in Geneva until Friday, after which he will return to Belfort to conduct his election campaign. He will return to Paris on Monday morning and then return to Geneva again on Tuesday morning, April 26th, to participate in the arms reduction conference work on Tuesday and Friday.

Geneva Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 21st: British Prime Minister MacDonald today overturned the pre-arranged plan for a tripartite meeting by U.S. Secretary of State Stimson. Stimson suddenly stopped at French Premier Tardieu's residence at 8:00 AM tomorrow. After a brief conversation, he drove to the British Prime Minister's residence, picked up MacDonald, and returned to his residence for secret talks. Around 11:00 AM, Tardieu and U.S. Representative Davis went to Stimson's place, planning for a two-hour tripartite meeting. However, MacDonald strongly advocated going to the arms reduction conference and left first.

Extreme Tension in the General Commission on Disarmament

The Future of the Conference Does Not Permit Optimism

Paul-Boncour Vigorously Attacks Italian-American Plans

Most Countries Support Simon's Proposals

Sato Surprisingly Speaks for France

Liu Wendao Delivers a Thought-Provoking Speech

Geneva Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 21st: Although the General Commission of the International Disarmament Conference continued its meeting today, the leaders of the four major powers did not attend initially. British Prime Minister MacDonald, French Premier Tardieu, and German Chancellor Brüning all had lengthy talks at Stimson's residence, hoping to find a compromise to overcome the current obstacles. The General Commission convened at 10:10 AM to continue discussing the Italian-American joint plan to conclude an international convention to abolish certain offensive weapons, and the resolution proposed yesterday by British Foreign Secretary Simon in support of the Italian-American plan. Canadian representative Penhale spoke first, enthusiastically supporting Simon's resolution. Norwegian representative Colban also strongly defended the Italian-American plan. The next to speak was French representative Paul-Boncour, who vehemently attacked the Italian-American plan and Simon's resolution, claiming that France could not accept the current form of the Italian-American plan because it would abolish the weapons that France intended to provide to the League of Nations forces. He also argued that organizing an international army, managed and used by the League of Nations with the weapons that Italy and America wanted to abolish, would be the greatest guarantee of world peace and security. The French believe that any arms reduction agreement should be based primarily on national security. French Premier Tardieu's hasty arrival in Geneva was because he saw that the Italian-American plan greatly threatened France's position. Therefore, Paul-Boncour's speech today was to defend this demand. Although his wording was tactful, his intention was firm and unwavering, indicating that France could not accept the abolition or restriction of any weapons until the General Commission accepted or rejected France's plan to arm the League of Nations with an international army. However, after France strongly rejected the British resolution, the conference fell into an extremely pessimistic state. The British Foreign Secretary's proposal was presented after much consultation and consideration, and its wording sought to avoid offending the French representative, so it guaranteed to abolish offensive weapons using only the most gentle methods, while not hindering other proposals. When the interpreters translated Paul-Boncour's lengthy speech, the listeners in the corridors whispered, fearing that the conference was not far from failure. Given the French attitude was so tough, it was expected that the conference would be forced to temporarily postpone voting on Simon's resolution and discuss the French plan, but many believed that the French proposal was doomed to failure. When Paul-Boncour was speaking, Simon looked very worried. When the interpreters were translating, the British Foreign Secretary immediately consulted with Italian Foreign Minister Grandi, looking quite anxious. U.S. Representative Gibson also joined in, and the three temporarily withdrew to another room to discuss how to proceed. At this time, German Chancellor Brüning arrived at the meeting and quietly took his seat. A few minutes later, British Prime Minister MacDonald also arrived and chatted with Litvinov, Sato, and the Persian representative Agha Khan. After the translation of Paul-Boncour's speech was completed, U.S. Representative Gibson took the stage to vigorously defend the Italian-American plan, especially insisting on the immediate abolition of artillery and tanks, declaring that although he was pleased that their goals had gained general approval, he still regretted that they had not agreed on the methods. He also replied to France's point that the Italian-American plan did not cover air and naval armaments, saying that they had already limited the navy, so this plan proposed reducing land armaments. Subsequently, he solemnly declared that the U.S. proposal did not hinder or prevent any country from negotiating any measures for the sake of security, and he affirmed that the U.S. supported Simon's resolution. Representatives from Ireland, South Africa, and Persia spoke in succession, all defending Simon's resolution. Representatives from Austria and Portugal followed, also expressing their support. Only Japanese representative Sato supported the French position, claiming that it was extremely difficult to determine whether a weapon was offensive or defensive, so there would inevitably be differences of opinion in selecting weapons to be banned. Chinese representative Liu Wendao followed with a thought-provoking and moving speech, advocating for Simon's resolution, declaring that the terrible destruction inflicted on his country's people by offensive weapons in recent months could serve as a lesson to the world, so he advocated abolishing all offensive weapons. After the Swedish representative spoke in support of Simon's position, the Italian representative delivered a passionate and eloquent speech, asking the entire assembly to vote unanimously in favor, declaring that Simon's resolution did not hinder the French plan.

Geneva Dispatch from Reuters on the 21st: Today, the Marquess of Londonderry held a luncheon here, and among the guests were representatives from the five countries participating in the arms reduction conference: British Prime Minister MacDonald, French Premier Tardieu, U.S. Secretary of State Stimson, German Chancellor Brüning, Italian Foreign Minister Grandi, and British Foreign Secretary Simon. The arms reduction conference has reached a critical juncture. Considering that Tardieu has suspended his important election campaign and Brüning has abandoned his domestic affairs to come here, one can imagine the seriousness of the situation. However, the world's major leaders have not yet been able to reach a resolution. Many parties now support Britain's arms reduction plan, which involves banning several of the most aggressive armaments. America, Germany, Italy, New Zealand, and Canada have agreed to the suggestion put forward by Simon. Canadian representative Penhale declared today that this was the first concrete suggestion after three months of talks. Britain's suggestion and France's plan are contradictory, as France advocates that all large bomber aircraft, heavy artillery, large submarines, and warships over 10,000 tons should be placed under the command of the League of Nations. Representatives from the Irish Free State, South Africa, India, Japan, the Netherlands, Australia, China, Switzerland, and Soviet Russia also supported Britain's suggestion. Romanian representative Titulescu, while not opposing Britain's suggestion, has presented a resolution on substantive armaments plans on behalf of fourteen countries. The conference has been extended to April 22nd.

Geneva Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 20th: In the General Commission of the International Disarmament Conference, British Foreign Secretary Simon proposed a resolution that supports Italy and America's abolition of offensive weapons and does not hinder the French plan to use offensive weapons exclusively for international armies. After suggesting that the principle of adopting the selection of certain types of weapons and banning their use by international convention be adopted, several small countries' representatives said that most of the proposals recently were not as thorough as Germany's proposal. The representative from Yugoslavia attacked the resolution put forward by Britain and proposed another resolution with a counter-proposal nature, requesting that ocean-going warships and submarines be abolished, that artillery and tanks be restricted, and that an agreement be made to make these weapons permanently available for use and direct control by the International League of Nations. Subsequently, Italian Foreign Minister Grandi and Lüford warmly supported the resolution proposed by Britain. As it was past noon, the meeting was adjourned and will continue tomorrow morning. At the beginning of this morning's meeting, Chairman Henderson put to a vote whether to continue the meeting this afternoon, but all the representatives were like primary school students, eager to get half a day off, and all opposed holding the meeting again in the afternoon.

Geneva Dispatch from Havas on the 20th: The first three months of the Disarmament Conference were a period of exploration. Now it has reached the center of the disarmament issue, or it can be said that the conference has fallen into the heart of the difficulty. However, this kind of difficulty is unavoidable for the conference. What is called the Commission is actually the General Assembly, because all national delegations have participated in it. In the past three days, the General Commission has discussed the most difficult issues, and how it resolves them is crucial to the success or failure of disarmament.

400,000 Red Army Troops Stationed in Siberia

Building 400 Bombers for Defense

| Russian Delegation Informs League of Nations Members |

Japanese Aggression Has Not Ceased

Tense Relations Between Russia and Japan

Geneva Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 19th: Today, a spokesperson for the Soviet Russian delegation informed members of the League of Nations that Moscow's attitude towards Japan is extremely firm. There are now 400,000 troops stationed in Siberia, and 400 bombers have been built to protect the territory and defend against aggression. Also, U.S. Secretary of State Stimson today denied the rumor that he had met with Soviet Russian Chief Representative and People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov.

Moscow Dispatch from Reuters on the 20th: Soviet Russian People's Committee Chairman Molotov said in a speech at the Trade Union Congress today that the facts have proved that the Japanese warlords and imperialists do have far-reaching aggressive intentions, not limited to seizing the three northeastern provinces. He also said that Soviet Russia's maintenance of peaceful relations with Japan is essential. The White Russians and the lackeys of the landlord capitalists and imperialist countries, as well as Chinese soldiers, who are willing to protect their interests at any cost, now all want to destroy Russian-Japanese relations. Molotov continued his speech, attacking the League of Nations and pointing out that the plans of the Far Eastern imperialists are related to the general staff of a certain Western capitalist country, saying that all things can show that the talk in the disarmament conference is only to cover up the true increase in armaments and the urgency of imperialist war. All of Russia's proposals have been rejected, so Russians have more necessity than before to work to maintain peace.

Riga Dispatch from Havas on the 20th: Judging from the editorials of Soviet Russian newspapers in recent days and the remarks of travelers arriving in Riga, it can be seen that Moscow is paying increasing attention to the possibility of a major dispute between itself and Japan. The most obvious thing is that Soviet Russian newspapers previously only attacked Japan's cunning, accusing White Russians of being used by Japan to engage in provocations and for all criminal acts. Soviet Russian newspapers, whenever they had the opportunity, were sure to tout Soviet Russian's peaceful ideas. The Soviet Russian press's attitude toward Japan was only like this before, but now they have changed their tune, saying that Soviet Russia will never allow its territory to be invaded, and when necessary, will resolutely resist aggressors. It is estimated that Soviet Russia foresees that in the future it will be forced by circumstances, or there will be a day when it cannot help but make concessions. The reason why it is currently adopting this attitude is precisely to take pre-emptive measures, so that even if it concedes in the future, it will not sacrifice too much. Currently, Moscow is eager for American assistance, so it is doing its best to exploit the conflict of interests between the United States and Japan in the Far East in order to obtain American cooperation. We can see this intention by browsing Soviet Russian newspapers.

Japanese Navy and Air Force Hold Offensive and Defensive Exercises

Two Aircraft Forced to Land in the Ocean

Tokyo Dispatch from Japan United Press on the 21st: The Yokosuka Naval Base held a basic naval exercise at 5:00 AM on the 20th, assuming that the enemy's base was on Hachijojima. Under the imaginary premise that the enemy was attacking Japanese territory, defensive combat actions were practiced. The Oppama, Tateyama, and Kasumigaura air units all participated, performing aerial combat in the skies near Hachijojima. During this exercise, reconnaissance aircraft No. 108 and another aircraft had engine failures and landed in the ocean. One of them was severely damaged, but the crew members were not injured. Also, a carrier-based fighter plane from Kasumigaura went missing, and its whereabouts are unknown.

German Authorities Express No Intention of Recognizing the Puppet State

Radio Station Communication is a Commercial Act

Berlin Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 20th: Today, German authorities made it clear that Germany has no intention of recognizing the Manchurian puppet state. Shenyang news claimed that the Shenyang radio station would soon be communicating with the German Nauen radio station, and this move could be interpreted as Germany de facto recognizing the new government of Manchuria. Therefore, German authorities denied this, saying that this interpretation was without basis. The communication between the two radio stations is purely a commercial act of the radio companies, no different from the agreed communication of the U.S. radio companies. It also solemnly declared that Germany will take the same attitude as the major powers on the recognition issue, with absolutely no intention of deviating from the crowd. Currently, none of the major powers have expressed a willingness to recognize the state.

South African Leader Proposes Abolishing the Oath of Allegiance for Officials

First Reading Passed by Parliament

Dublin Dispatch from the National News Agency on the 20th: The Irish Free State Parliament today allowed the new Irish head of state, Éamon de Valera, to present a bill to Parliament to abolish the oath of allegiance to the British monarch taken by Irish officials upon taking office. The bill immediately passed its first reading in Parliament today without a vote. Éamon de Valera has strongly opposed this oath of allegiance to the British monarch for decades during the revolution. Now, after taking office as head of state, he has begun to attack this oath ceremony. In the future, the British side will definitely criticize it, so the future is still unpredictable.

Important News

Ma Zhanshan's Telegram to the Investigation Team Exposes Japanese Conspiracy

Detailed Account of On-the-Ground Experiences Over Two Months

Hoping That the Investigation Team Will Make an Honest Report

After arriving in Heihe, Ma Zhanshan telegraphed the entire country, reporting that he would continue to resist Japan. At the same time, he also sent a telegram to the League of Nations Investigation Team. The original text is as follows:

Transmitted from Shanghai China Telegraph via Luoyang National Government, for the perusal of Director Zhang, Pacification Headquarters in Beiping. I am planning to send a telegram to the League of Nations Investigation Team, and I respectfully request that it be translated and forwarded. Since the Manchurian people have mixed with our Han people, for three hundred years, they have lived in Manchuria and lived in peace. Politics, culture, customs, language, and religion are all the same. Therefore, the political revolution of 1910, although it overthrew the Qing government and changed to a republic, there was not the slightest expression of hatred between the Han people and the Manchurian people. Moreover, the distinction in names between Manchurians and Han people also disappeared invisibly. This is generally seen and heard by people around the world who are slightly familiar with the situation in China, and it is certainly not my personal opinion. Therefore, the so-called Manchurians and Manchuria have become historical terms, and there is no value in citing them today. However, the Japanese must want to use them as a rare commodity, secretly using this old term in the dictionary to divide our nation and seize our land. It is unimaginable that in the 20th century, in the civilized world, there are still behaviors that despise international justice and are brutally inhumane, which is a fuse for destroying peace in East Asia. Article 10 of the League of Nations Covenant has a provision that members of the League of Nations are responsible for respecting and maintaining the territorial integrity of all members of the League of Nations. Also, the Washington Nine-Power Treaty of 1922 has provisions to guarantee China's territorial and administrative integrity and the open door and equal opportunity in the three northeastern provinces. These all made it difficult for Japan to annex the three northeastern provinces, so it used the name of national self-determination and, by means of kidnapping, forcibly robbed the abdicated Emperor Puyi, escorting him from Tianjin to Lushun. It also threatened and lured the original officials of the three northeastern provinces to stage a farce. Puyi tried to commit suicide with medicine many times on the way, but was discovered and stopped by the Japanese who were monitoring him. He could not die, and his situation was also miserable. I, Ma Zhanshan, was ordered by the National Government to serve as Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government and Deputy Commander of the Northeastern Border Defense Army stationed in Jiang. I am responsible for the defense of Heilongjiang Province. However, since the September 18th Incident last year, the Japanese army successively occupied Liaoning and Jilin provinces, and then deliberately plotted against Heilongjiang. Under the pretext of repairing the Nenjiang Bridge, it attacked our army by surprise. I, Ma Zhanshan, immediately took the front line and tried to defend myself. We exchanged fire for a period of two weeks. Due to the poor quality of weapons and the exhaustion of ammunition, we retreated to Hailun. However, the headquarters of the Japanese army repeatedly sent people to say that the military and political authorities of Liaoning and Jilin provinces had now agreed on a method for organizing new administrations in the two provinces. When the new administrations were established, Japan would withdraw its troops immediately and would never interfere in administration. Only Heilongjiang Province is an obstacle, causing the entire situation to be restless. In order to restore the security of the three provinces, I would return to Heilongjiang and unconditionally return the Heilongjiang government. After arriving in the province, the Japanese army would immediately withdraw, etc. At the same time, the puppet heads of Liaoning and Jilin provinces, under the instruction of the Japanese, sent people to say that the new administration was indeed independent in nature. Therefore, I agreed to return to the province in order to observe the situation and make a decision. Unexpectedly, after entering the province, the Japanese, as a dignified country, disregarded good faith and immediately broke their promise. Not only did they not withdraw a single soldier, but they also used the pretext of the unity of the three provinces to establish a puppet state, so as to implement the steps for annexation. Therefore, the positions of administrative committee member, Heilongjiang provincial governor, and army chief of staff were fabricated one after another. I, Ma Zhanshan, was able to take this opportunity to observe the inner workings of the Japanese aggressors and the truth of the puppet state, so as to contribute it to your association, which is the only organization for maintaining world peace and advocating international justice. This is also a great fortune in misfortune. I will now disclose the summary of my diary of my actual experience over the past month to your investigation team for reference. Please review it. On February 16th, I reluctantly complied with the Japanese request and went to Liaoning by plane to attend a meeting. On February 17th, I met with Honjo Shigeru, who claimed that the Japanese army had occupied most of the three northeastern provinces, and only a small part of Heilongjiang and Jilin was extremely difficult to resist. He requested that I cooperate with the Japanese. That evening, a meeting was held at Zhao Xinbo's residence. All the plans I proposed to abolish the establishment of the puppet state were sternly rejected by Itagaki of the Japanese side. The meeting ended without results that day. On February 18th, I pretended to be sick and returned to Hailun by car. According to Zhao Zhongren's report, on the 19th, the Japanese army headquarters ordered Zhang Jinghui and Zhao Zhongren to lead twelve puppet representatives from the three provinces of Jilin, Heilongjiang who had been bribed by the Japanese to go to Dalian to entreat Puyi to be the puppet head, and instructed Puyi to decline three times. The representatives pleaded three times before finally accepting the order. On March 8th, the Japanese repeatedly invited me to Changchun. I was planning to find an excuse to shirk, but I was afraid that it would cause suspicion, so I had no choice but to go to Changchun to welcome Puyi. On the 9th, Puyi assumed the position of puppet head. All the ceremonies were presided over by the Japanese. A puppet appeared on the stage, and this is what it means. The most hateful thing is that Honjo Shigeru came to Changchun to monitor Puyi's inauguration and ordered Puyi to respectfully greet him at the east station. After repeated requests, some face was saved, and it was agreed that the puppet Prime Minister Zheng Xiaoxu would represent him. This shows that Honjo really regarded himself as the governor-general, and what he called coexistence and co-prosperity was completely a deceptive trick. On March 10th, the Japanese side, through Komai and Itagaki, held a puppet state council meeting with orders from the Japanese military department. At the same time, it also announced that the Manchurian puppet government would set up a chief of general affairs, who would be filled by a Japanese and would be in charge of all real powers in the various departments. All government orders could not be executed without the signature and seal of the puppet chief of general affairs. On March 11th, Colonel Staff Officer Itagaki and Puppet Chief of General Affairs Komai declared at the puppet state council meeting that the Japanese government originally intended to participate in half of the officials in the new government and the puppet provincial governments, but now they are trying their best to reduce it, and only added one hundred and several dozen Japanese to the new government in Changchun. It was also said that Japanese people residing in the three northeastern provinces would belong to the nationality of the new country, and all public rights would be enjoyed equally with the Manchurians. As for whether they would renounce Japanese nationality, they would have the right to weigh it, and others would not be allowed to interfere. It was also decided that the chiefs of general affairs and police affairs departments to be filled by Japanese in Liaoning and Jilin provinces would be assigned to be in charge of all real powers in the respective provinces. All government orders could not be implemented without their signature and seal. It was also agreed that the assignment of Heilongjiang province would be postponed for three months. On March 16th, Honjo Shigeru came to Qiqihar and inspected the Daxing area. During the conversation on the way, (1) the entire Japanese nation had made up its mind and would rather pay any sacrifice than give up the three northeastern provinces. (2) Anyone who opposed the new government would be the sole responsibility of the Japanese army to eliminate completely. (3) If any third country came out to interfere, it had made the final determination to declare war. (4) Regarding all government orders, they could be carried out step by step, but they had to be approved by the local Japanese military department and special service agencies before they could be implemented. Also, the puppet State Council decided that (1) all land in the northeast that had been released, if the location was for officials or warlords, would be confiscated in full. If the number of mu of civilians was large, half of them would be purchased at the official price and all would be taken back by the puppet state for use by the Japanese government for immigration purposes. (2) The Hulan-Hai Railway is the hub of Heilongjiang Province's grain transportation. The Japanese and Zhang Jinghui signed a contract, forcibly mortgaging it for 3 million yuan at a tenth of its price, with a term of 50 years, which is no different from permanent occupation. I fear that Ma Zhanshan will not recognize it.

News Summary

Signing of Supplementary Commercial Treaty: Despite strong refusals, the puppet state's Ministry of Transportation is being forced to proceed. (3) Planning to establish the puppet state's "Manzhou Bank" using the model of the Bank of Korea, with the aim of manipulating finances and extracting wealth from us. (4) Destroying our country's schools and invading our culture. In all schools, in addition to stationing troops, all of our original, nationally-approved textbooks at all levels that inspire patriotism are being revised and supplemented with pro-Japanese ideas, in order to eliminate our nation. Furthermore, Doihara, head of the Harbin Special Service Agency, and Suzuki, commander of the brigade, have stated that since Japan has obtained the three eastern provinces, once military expenses are sufficient, they will use them as a source for war strategies, first invading Soviet Russia to the north, then resisting the United States to the east, and gradually targeting other countries. The above are the experiences and circumstances personally witnessed by Ma Zhanshan. Currently, each county in the two provinces of Liaoning and Jilin has two Japanese assigned to handle special affairs. Nothing can be implemented without their permission. All newspapers, telegrams, and telephones in the three eastern provinces are controlled behind the scenes by the Japanese, and newspapers have no true public opinion except to comply with Japanese intentions. Now that the esteemed investigation team is about to arrive in the east, the Japanese are warning intellectuals that anyone with speech unfavorable to Japan will be dealt with decisively. Anyone who opposes Japan is being secretly arrested and killed in their homes by the Japanese at night, and their families are warned that if they leak the news, they will face the same fate. Yan Tingrui, Zhang Kui'en, and others have all been killed. The so-called public opinion celebrating the establishment of the puppet state in the three eastern provinces is all fabricated by the Japanese. They are now also buying off unscrupulous and treacherous people to promote their virtuous rule. The above is what Ma Zhanshan has learned from his investigation. Now that the esteemed investigation team has arrived in our country, Ma Zhanshan, for the sake of national salvation, has resolutely risked the greatest danger and devised a plan to escape from Qiqihar, which is under strict surveillance by the Japanese army, and secretly come to Heihe, to carry out the duties of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government. All political affairs are carried out in accordance with the central government, and the truth of the organization of the puppet state of Manchukuo is presented to the esteemed investigation team, which has been specially commissioned to come to China, and to people all over the world who want to know the truth. Now, with the utmost sincerity, I swear and declare: Not a single person in our three eastern provinces is willing to separate from our country and live outside of it. Even the officials now working in the puppet government are under severe surveillance by the Japanese army and have lost their freedom. Please pay special attention to this and conduct an actual investigation so that an honest report can be made. Only then can the future of world peace be guaranteed, and the esteemed investigation team's contribution to world humanity will be eternally immortalized. Furthermore, Ma Zhanshan has more to say: Last autumn, hundreds of our overseas Chinese were killed in Korea, and property losses amounted to millions. But did our national government ever use the pretext of protecting overseas Chinese to send a single soldier or general into Korea? In recent years, Japanese residents in our country have not faced any danger, but their government has brazenly sent troops to invade our eastern provinces and attack Shanghai, using the pretext of protecting the lives and property of its residents. Comparing the two, the upholders of justice in the world will have their own opinions. Moreover, Japanese residents are spread throughout the countries of the five continents. If their government sometimes also uses the pretext of protecting the interests of its residents to send troops and generals to invade the places where its residents live, then we are truly in danger of world peace. I hope the esteemed investigation team will consider this carefully. In addition to sending a direct telegram to our country's representative Yan in Geneva, this notice is hereby issued. Sincerely, Ma Zhanshan, Chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, from Heihe.

A Pessimistic View on Manchu-Mongolian Immigration by the Japanese Newspaper

The Kobe Shimbun published an editorial on the 12th stating that the Ministry of Colonial Affairs' planned Manchu-Mongolian immigration project aims to relocate 100,000 households, or 500,000 people, within ten years. This year, it plans to relocate 640 households, about 3,000 people, with a budget of 3 million yuan, which was submitted to the extraordinary session of the parliament in May. However, the Ministry of Finance, citing a lack of funds, has refused to approve it and has expressed pessimism about the possibility of success of the Manchu-Mongolian immigration. The question of whether relocating the excess population to the vast Manchu-Mongolian region will be beneficial in terms of labor competition remains doubtful. If the government is already facing difficulties in spending 3 million yuan, then the planned immigration of 500,000 people over ten years may not be realized annually. It should be noted that Chinese laborers in Manchuria can live on coarse clothing and simple food with low wages. It would be impossible for our people (Japanese) to live this way. In addition, the harsh climate and unsuitable land in Manchu-Mongolia pose significant problems for immigration. Therefore, implementing a large-scale immigration plan without careful consideration is ignorant and clueless. Furthermore, after the Russo-Japanese War, our country's immigration associations flourished, and immigration was encouraged by all parties, but the results were disastrous. Therefore, the future of immigration today, so-called immigrants, are really nothing but abandoned people.

Academic Circles in Shanghai Oppose the Increase in Postage for Books

Since the Ministry of Communications announced the method of increasing postage, postal workers and students in Peiping have telegraphed their opposition, which has been repeatedly reported in various newspapers. Academic circles in Shanghai, including Liu Zhan'en, Ou Yuanhuai, Wu Jingtai, Cao Huiqun, Hu Dunfu, Chen Heqin, Huang Yanpei, Li Zhaohuan, Jiang Hengyuan, Wang Jin, etc., also believe that the method of increasing postage for books is enough to hinder the progress of our country's culture, and have specially telegraphed the Executive Yuan to express their opposition. The original telegram and original presentation are now found below.

Telegram to the Executive Yuan of the National Government: Shanghai newspapers report that the postage increase method for books, etc., proposed by the Ministry of Communications is extremely harsh and detailed, and it also regards provinces such as Gansu, Shaanxi, Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou as outside the pale of civilization, with particularly heavy increases. This is detrimental to the construction of promoting cultural development and the frontiers. Recently, the government has spent huge sums to promote aviation in the northwest, so why should postage for books in the border provinces be particularly increased? It is truly incomprehensible. It is requested that the Ministry of Communications be ordered to abolish the said method and maintain the old plan. We cannot bear to hope. In addition to a separate presentation, we first telegraph to inform you.

Presentation: The presentation is for the heavy increase in postage for books, and we earnestly request that the old plan be maintained in order to lighten the burden and provide funds for promotion. We have secretly read the Shen Bao published on April 17 of this year, the method of increasing postage, where postage for letters, postcards, books, printed matter, etc., has all been increased. Among them, the regulations for increasing postage for books and printed matter are extremely harsh and detailed, and for the five provinces of Gansu, Shaanxi, Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou, they have been increased by two to three times. Zhan, etc., believe that the matter is of great importance to the future of our country's education and culture, and they dare not fail to contribute their humble opinions for consideration. According to the postage list of the Republic of China in 1925 and the fee increase notice in 1931, all books and printed matter were sent as ordinary mail. Except for Mongolia and Xinjiang, there were no differences in the postage charged between provinces. This time, the method of sending parcels in the past is applied to books, and the adjacent provinces and non-adjacent provinces, the places where rails are connected and the places where they are not connected, are all stipulated separately. As a result, postage has invariably increased. At a time when our country's cultural and educational undertakings need to be promoted vigorously, this method of increasing postage is enough to increase the burden of reading for the people of the whole country, and it will have a great impact on the promotion of the cultural and educational undertakings of the whole country. This is because we have to ask to maintain the old plan when observing on the general cultural and educational undertakings of the whole country. In addition, according to the previous postal regulations, except for Mongolia and Xinjiang, the postal charges for other provinces were the same throughout the country, with no differences. The explanation of this increase method is that in addition to Mongolia and Xinjiang remaining the same, Gansu, (Qinghai, Ningxia,) Shaanxi, Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou, etc., are also listed as exceptions, and the postage for sending books and printed matter in these five provinces has been increased by two to three times. The development of the west is an important plan for the construction of our country, and the closed customs and difficult livelihoods of the western provinces are also a fact that everyone can see. Then, promoting the education of the people of these provinces and reducing the burden of the people of these provinces is even more important. Recently, the government has spent huge sums to promote aviation in the northwest, so why should postage for books in the border provinces be particularly increased? It seems to be inconsistent with the government's policy of developing the interior. This is also because we have to ask to maintain the old plan when observing on the active construction of the western provinces. Zhan En, etc., believe that promoting the progress of the cultural and educational undertakings of the whole country, and developing the frontiers with closed customs and difficult livelihoods, are all urgent tasks for our country at present. Now, in the period of political tutelage, the responsibilities of the government lie in actively promoting them. If the method of increasing postage is actually implemented, the government's annual income can be increased, but the important undertakings of promoting national culture and education, and developing the frontiers, will inevitably be greatly affected. Zhan En, etc., are in danger and cannot remain silent. It is reasonable to prepare a document and request your approval and implementation, which is really for the public good. Respectfully submitted to Wang, the President of the Executive Yuan of the National Government.

Taxpayers' Association Writes to the Municipal Council to Request Lenient Enforcement Against Street Vendors

The Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Public Concession wrote to the Municipal Council yesterday, saying, "Regarding the matter of cracking down on street vendors, this association believes that it should be lenient. According to the letters from the street vendors, thousands of street vendors depend on selling goods on the roads for a living. They know to restrain themselves in terms of traffic order and have never caused any hindrance. However, the police often drive them away, arrest them, and impose fines. The suffering of the street vendors is extremely deep and great. Last year, fortunately, Director Yu Zhiqing took pity on the livelihoods of the common people and strongly persuaded the Municipal Council to make a comeback, benefiting the poor and creating happiness for society, which was a great merit. Now that the Shanghai war has temporarily subsided, the livelihoods of the people are in a very difficult situation. If the Concession authorities are really concerned about the fundamental security of the area, they should find ways to maintain the livelihoods of the poor, but instead, they are once again strictly cracking down on them. This is no different from forcing the common people to embark on a dangerous path. If the street vendors have no way to make a living and mistakenly take a step down the wrong path, it will inevitably have a great impact on the security of the Concession. Therefore, we have no choice but to request that your association consider the difficulty of the street vendors' lives and strongly request the Concession authorities to be lenient, directly saving the lives of thousands of people, which will also maintain the security of the Concession. We are extremely grateful and humbly request your understanding." In response, we request that your council consider the matter carefully, not simply focusing on formalities and creating more hidden dangers.

Unemployment Relief Fund Management Committee Established Yesterday

Guo Shun, Wang Yansong, and Zhu Wenqi Elected as Executive Directors

Designation of China and Five Other Banks to Collect Donations on Behalf

The Shanghai War Zone Unemployment Relief Association, organized by the Social Affairs Bureau and others, has begun to raise funds after the establishment of the Fundraising Committee. The Management Committee has also appointed Xu Shiying, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Shi Liangcai, Huang Jinrong, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Guo Shun, Ye Huijun, Xu Jiqin, Pei Yunqing, Wen Lanting, Lin Kanghou, Min Ruisheng, Fu Xiaoan, Zhu Wenqi, etc., as members. Yesterday at noon, Mai Chaochu of the Social Affairs Bureau, together with Zhu Wenqi, director of the Economic Division of the Association, invited all the Management Committee members at the Wewei Dining Hall on the 9th floor of the YMCA. More than ten people, including Xu Shiying, Guo Shun, Wen Lanting, and Pei Yunqing, formally announced the establishment on the spot. Secretary Zhang Zhenyuan attended and reported. Guo Shun, Wang Yansong, and Zhu Wenqi were elected as executive directors on the spot, and the following resolutions were made: (1) Designating five banks, including the Bank of China, Central Bank, Bank of Shanghai, Silk Industry Bank, and Zhonghui Bank, as collection points for donations, which will be coordinated by Committee Member Zhu Wenqi. (2) Appointing two national accountants, Xi Yushu and Wang Sifang, to audit the receipts and expenditures of donations to ensure transparency. The 5th Executive Committee meeting was held at 2:00 PM on the same day. After the reports were given by each division, the discussion focused on the implementation of temporary relief matters. It was resolved to reserve the decision and wait until a sufficient amount of funds has been raised before discussing methods.

Second Special District Court Burned a Large Batch of Drugs Yesterday

The Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Court, since its establishment in August last year, has set a rule to burn all confiscated contraband such as opium, lamps, guns, red and white pills, etc., once every three months. The first session was burned on November 14 last year. Yesterday was the date of the second session of drug destruction, which consisted of opium and drugs confiscated during the five months from November last year to March this year, and gambling paraphernalia confiscated during the six months from August last year to January this year, such as pai gow tiles, dice, lottery tickets, etc. In advance, the president of the court, Ying Shi, and the chief prosecutor, Chen Beisan, submitted a report to the Ministry of Justice and the Higher Third Branch Court and invited representatives from various agencies to supervise the event. Yesterday at noon, the president of the court first sent personnel to set up a venue in the open space in front of the staff dormitory of the Second Special District Prison next door to the court. A shed was built, and tables and chairs were placed. Meanwhile, Feng Meixue, the director of the confiscated goods warehouse, sent people to arrange all the drugs and gambling paraphernalia piece by piece on both sides of the venue, and prepared firewood, kerosene, salt, and other ignition materials. Yang Zhaoqi, the section chief of the Ministry of Justice, and Li Yuanxi, a clerk, came to Shanghai to supervise the event. Tang Zaili, the secretary of the Higher Third Branch Court, and Lin Xi, the chief secretary of the Higher Third Branch Prosecutor's Office, supervised the event. At 2:30 PM, representatives from various agencies arrived one after another. Xu Shaoxiu of the Shanghai Municipal Government, Ye Hongji of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Tuan Youchang of the Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office, Zhang Fuzai of the Social Affairs Bureau, Gong Yushuo of the Public Security Bureau, Xu Zuyin of the Higher Second Branch Court, Zhu Huanwen of the Higher Second Branch Prosecutor's Office, Guo Wei of the First Special District Court, Qian of the Prosecutor's Office of the First Special District Court, Wang Xun of the Shanghai District Court, Yang Qi of the Prosecutor's Office of the District Court, Li Ruzhang of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Zhou Chufang and Duan Zhen'e of the China Anti-Drug Association, Li Daiyi (transliteration), the Western detective of the French Concession Police Department, Translator Cao Huanwen, lawyers Fei Xizhen and Gu Shoux, and representatives from the Shanghai County Government and the Shanghai Bar Association were received and seated by President Ying, Chief Chen, and Secretary-General Xiao Jinfang, and were given a list of drugs and gambling paraphernalia, one copy for each representative, totaling four copies. At 3:00 PM, the secretaries and constables executing the event on the spot moved the drugs piece by piece to the front of the seats. After each representative inspected and verified the seals, they immediately threw the drugs into the fire in the firewood pile on the spot, poured kerosene on them, and added salt. The burning lasted for two hours before it was completed. A total of 272 guns, several hundred pounds of opium and red and white pills, and countless smoking lamps, smoking trays, smoking rods, lottery tickets, dominoes, etc., were burned. At 5:30 PM, the representatives took their leave and dispersed.

Three Hemp Bags of Opium Intercepted

Weighing a Total of 273 Jin

Western Constable No. 121 and Chinese Constable No. 556 of the French Concession patrolled Huangpu Beach in front of the Taikoo Wharf on the night of the 20th and saw three Chinese walking out of Xin Yong'an Street towards the wharf. A No. 12204 car from the Nanyang Motor Company drove from Gongguan Road and stopped at the wharf. A Chinese jumped out and ordered the previous Chinese to shoulder three hemp bags containing goods outside the wharf, seemingly wanting to load them onto the car. They were acting suspiciously. When the constables went forward to inspect them, the car immediately drove off and fled, and the three who carried the bags also abandoned the bags and ran away. The constables went forward to inspect the bags and found that they were all opium. They immediately took them to the police station, where they were weighed and found to be 273 jin. Yesterday, they were sent to the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court. Lawyer Gu Shoux of the police station stated that the opium in the three ownerless hemp bags was discovered by the patrolmen on Huangpu Beach and requested that it be confiscated first, and that the person who smuggled it be prosecuted after he has been identified. Western Constable No. 121 and Chinese Constable No. 556 reported the circumstances of the discovery. Judge Li Changnian ordered the opium to be confiscated and sent to the confiscated goods warehouse, pending investigation of the smuggler.

Striving for Tap Water Leads to the Death of a Woman

Court Conducts Preliminary Examination

Police Still Need to Investigate

Guo, 42 years old, wife of Shao Mingde, a Henan native who buys and sells used goods at No. 25 Xixiang Lane, Lafayette Road in the French Concession, went to the public tap inside the alley to draw water at 5:15 PM on the 20th. She argued with Li Zhang, a young woman from Jiangbei living at No. 30 of the same lane, over who would draw water first. Li Zhang grabbed Guo's hair and beat her, with accomplices assisting, causing Guo to be injured and fall to the ground, dying instantly. The assailants scattered and fled. Shao Mingde, the deceased's husband, upon learning of this, reported it to the police. Detective Mao Jingen and detective Bao Wang Licheng arrested Li Zhang and took her to the police station. However, the accomplices were nowhere to be found. The body was taken to the autopsy room of Tongren Fuyuan Branch for examination. On Sunday, Prosecutor Wu Xiaoke of the Second Special Court was requested to come to the scene to confirm that the death was caused by the beating. Because the deceased's husband claimed he could not afford to handle the funeral arrangements, the official instructed that the body be handed over to Tongren Fuyuan Hall for funeral and burial. After the examination, the police immediately escorted Li Zhang to the First Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. Police lawyer Gu Shouxi explained the situation and filed charges according to Article 296 of the Criminal Law, requesting a postponement for further investigation. Shao Mingde, the deceased's husband, also recounted the tragic circumstances of his wife's beating. Judge Li Changnian briefly questioned the defendant and then ordered a postponement for continued questioning on May 2nd. The defendant was taken into custody.

Ferryboat Violently Hit by a Vessel

Four People Fall into the Water

Rescued by the Lissen

At 12:00 PM on the 20th, Yang Gengen and Zhang Abing were rowing a ferryboat to transport passengers across the Huangpu River in Dongjiadu. At that time, a vessel with the registration number 4964, steered by Du, was sailing with the wind. It struck the ferryboat, causing the boat and passengers to fall into the water. Upon realizing the accident, the vessel immediately sped away. Fortunately, Luo Abing and all the crew of the Lissen, which belongs to the Huangpu River Dredging Bureau, immediately deployed lifeboats and provided assistance, rescuing all those who fell into the water, allowing them to survive. They also chased the vessel that caused the accident to Gaochang Temple before capturing it. They were then handed over to the Water Patrol Team for investigation. The righteous and courageous actions of the Lissen crew are commendable.

Methods for Film Censorship Committee to Inspect Films in Shanghai

The Shanghai Film Association requested the Film Censorship Committee to send personnel to Shanghai to review new films during the period when traffic between Beijing and Shanghai is disrupted. This request was forwarded to the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Interior for instructions. In addition to dispatching personnel from both ministries, together with instructors from the Central Propaganda Committee, to take the first bus from Beijing to Hangzhou on the 21st and arrive in Shanghai around the 22nd to inspect new films, the following is a summary of the methods approved by the two ministries: (1) If traffic between Beijing and Shanghai has not resumed by May 31st of this year, the association may send personnel to Shanghai twice for inspection. Each time, the association shall designate one member from the Central Propaganda Committee and one member from the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Interior who also serve as members of the association to be stationed in Shanghai for inspection, limited to five days. During this period, both Chinese and foreign film companies may apply for their new films to be reviewed. After approval by these members, a temporary permit will be issued, allowing the film to be screened in designated cinemas for three to seven days. Upon expiration, the respective companies shall transport the original film to the capital to apply to the association for formal inspection. This temporary measure shall cease by May 31st of this year at the latest and shall not be taken as a precedent. (2) For each film inspected in Shanghai, the applicant shall pay a special inspection fee, the amount of which shall be 40% of the original inspection fee (ten yuan for every 500 meters, with any portion less than 500 meters counted as 500 meters). (3) If train service between Beijing and Shanghai resumes as normal before May 31st of this year, this temporary measure shall be terminated in advance.

Central Bank Inspection Report

No. 122

The 122nd Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserve of the Central Bank states that, in accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, the committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of convertible banknotes by the bank. On April 20, 1932, Supervisor Yu Yiqing conducted the 122nd inspection at the bank's Issuance Bureau. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: Silver dollars 27,200,554, including silver dollar notes 24,510,352 and subsidiary currency notes 2,695,102. Total amount of reserve funds for convertible banknotes: Silver dollars 27,200,554, including cash reserve in silver dollars 21,596,182. This cash reserve includes 18,516,503.45 yuan stored in the bank's Issuance Vault, 1,367,107 yuan stored in branches in various ports, and 1,663,571.55 yuan deposited with other banks. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 5,600,9272 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold convertible banknotes issued: 375,000 customs gold units. Total amount of reserve funds for customs gold convertible banknotes: 375,000 customs gold units. This reserve fund includes US$150,000 deposited with other banks in this port, converted to customs gold at the fixed price of 40, as stated above. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank's convertible banknote regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guaranteed reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guaranteed reserve is less than 40%, which is consistent with the regulations. This report is hereby submitted. Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank of China, April 20, 1932.

Notorious Child Abductor Li Sanguan Captured

Conspiring with Gu Qiaosheng to Lure a Boy from Liuhe to Shanghai

The notorious child abductor Li Sanguan, a native of Zha Pu, usually colludes with accomplices to lure boys and girls from various rural Fujian areas and sell them in Xiamen, Fujian. Recently, Li, along with accomplice Gu Qiaosheng, abducted a boy named Sheng Danan from Liuhe. They brought him to Shanghai and hid him in the Gongxing Inn in Cunshan Lane, Shangshi Guanqiao, intending to ship him to Xiamen for sale. However, their plan was discovered. At around 9:00 PM the night before last, someone secretly reported this to the local police station in District One, requesting an arrest. Upon receiving the report, District Chief Wang ordered squad leader Dong Mingde and other detectives to go to the inn, where they arrested the child abductors Li Sanguan and Gu Qiaosheng, and brought the abducted boy Sheng Danan back to the district. During the preliminary interrogation by the district chief, Sheng Danan claimed to be five years old, from Jiaxing, and that his father opened a shoe store in Liuhe. He could not provide further details. When questioned, Li Sanguan confessed to being 39 years old and admitted to abducting Sheng Danan with the intention of selling him in Xiamen. He also confessed to numerous previous cases of abducting and selling boys and girls. When questioned, Gu Qiaosheng, 43 years old, gave the same confession as Li. As the case involved trafficking in persons, it was ordered that a written report be prepared and submitted to the bureau for further investigation.

Free Talk

Proposal to Build Xiaode Road

Bo Han

American aviator Xiaode rose up angrily to protect world peace. He fought Japanese aircraft in the skies of Jinshan, and finally died in the wilderness because he was outnumbered. Our government, to express respect and gratitude, consulted Xiaode's mother and publicly buried Xiaode's remains in Hongqiao, Shanghai. Xiaode's mother traveled across the ocean to personally attend the grand ceremony. Thus, the two great republics facing each other on the east and west coasts of the Pacific Ocean will see their friendship and international relations strengthened. The spiritual and material cooperation between China and the United States did not begin today. Historical records bear this out. The names of the streets in Shanghai are mostly named after figures related to Chinese history. There are many who have contributed to our country. If we can think of the meaning behind the names when we travel, we should be able to feel the admiration or emotion for our predecessors. Roads such as Lahn Road, Hart Road, Scott Road, and Aierjin all represent a Westerner in modern times, each with their own deeds to study. Furthermore, in China, those who have military achievements are Major Gordon and General Ward, one British and one American, who both shine in our history. Among them, Ward's deeds are particularly prominent. Ward led the Changsheng Army with thousands of soldiers, fought in the southeast, and settled Shanghai. He later died in Songjiang. The capital issued an order to commend him and build a temple for him, with sacrifices in spring and autumn. Ward is the only foreigner with blue eyes and yellow beard who receives sacrifices from China. However, Ward and Gordon were raised by the Manchus to pacify Hong and Yang, which was still Chinese killing Chinese. How can it be compared to Xiaode, who resented the Japanese and mourned the poisoning of the innocent? He raised his arms and did not care for his own safety, defending international justice for the world as a neutral person and eradicating the powerful. His fame cannot be compared with Ward. Now that Shanghai already has roads such as Gordon Road and Ward Road, I believe that a major thoroughfare should be selected in the newly developed area of ​​western Shanghai and given a good name to show permanent observation. As for the soldiers who died in our country this time, road names should also be gradually added to make them immortal.

Recording Precious Screens in the Old Palace

Chen Yichan, an old man from Shu, is skilled in cypress matters and proficient in appraisal. Recently, he was visiting Shanghai. Yesterday I passed by his residence, and he had just acquired a treasure-inlaid screen from the old palace. After I had the opportunity to observe it, I was secretly delighted that Zuo had no limit. Record it to tell the readers.

This screen has a total of eight panels. It is nine feet high and about two feet wide. The screen frame is made of rosewood. The middle is plated with carved lacquer panels. The lacquer panels are inlaid with precious stones, jade, coral, colored jade, etc. The precious stones are all carved into objects. Everything is complete, including people, objects, birds, animals, flowers, grass, insects, and fish. The colors are red, green, blue, and purple. The eyes are fascinated by the five colors. There are eight stories on the screen, including the Three Heroes of the Wind and Dust, Su Wu Herding Sheep, Taibai Drunk, Jiemo Writing Poems, Clear Sky Bathing Ducks, Yinghong Touring the Garden, Asking the Way Under Pine Trees, and Asking Qiao After the Horse. The precious stones are all based on their color and size, and describe the shapes of various objects. It is extremely skillful and captures the essence of the craftsman. Especially Taibai in the Taibai Drunk Wine and the eminent monk under the pine tree. One is drowsy with drunkenness, and the other is solemn. The eminent monk's cassock is made of rubies, which is lifelike. It is amazing.

The screen was made during the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty. It was originally stored in the forbidden palace. Later, Gaozong gave it to his teacher Liu. This object was passed down to the people. Recently, a member of Liu's family brought it to Shanghai. Chan Weng bought it with a lot of money. Objects get their masters. No wonder Chan Weng is happy. I heard that the old man will put this screen in a high study for art critics to appreciate. This journal will compile and print a large 60th anniversary special issue on April 30th. I hope that all fellow writers will contribute their works. Whether it is anecdotes, stories, legends, novels, miscellaneous feelings, essays, illustrations, etc., all are welcome. The number of words per article is still 500 words. Please send it before the 29th of this month. Once recorded, the remuneration will be generous.

Free Talk Editorial Department

The Shanghai War and Military Equipment (16) One, Tibet

Unmanned aircraft means aircraft that do not require human power and are equipped with radio driving. After Marconi invented radio telegraph in 1897, the British physicist Wilson created unmanned radio-controlled automatic boats. Later, due to the advancement of electricity, it was renewed every day and gradually reached practical application. However, although this type of aircraft has not yet appeared, it is said that military strategists have researched it to success. As modern military equipment advances, it becomes more and more peculiar. In terms of radio technology used in the military, such as artillery equipment, sound source positioning machines for reconnaissance of enemy situations, rotating machines, panorama telescope theodolites. Various measuring machines. Wired and wireless telegraph and telephone in communication materials. Invisible light communication devices for secret communication. Optical telephone signal machine. And the use of invisible light to warn positions can find targets. Perspective cameras for taking smoke and fog, etc. Finding camouflage and electric current Anti-aircraft electrical listening devices for wire nets. Air lighting. And various power machines, etc. There are countless types of military applications that use electro-optics. For example, the anti-aircraft guns used recently can fire a large number of bullets in an instant to attack enemy aircraft. This is due to the electrical linkage, which enables observers to calculate on the machine. Even on dark nights and thick fog, observation can be done with the help of airborne acoustic listening devices and spotlights. With the advancement of radio telegraph, such as short-wave, ultra-short-wave, high-speed communication and heavy communication, etc., the invention of electrical photography and television devices for military use is gradually being developed. Therefore, the rear command post can use electrical photography and television methods to understand the situation in front. There are also direction detectors to detect the configuration of enemy communication stations and infer the enemy's deployment. Because of the sharpness of various electro-optical effects and scientific craftsmanship, the completion of unmanned aircraft is promoted to meet the needs of the times.

National Hatred and Family Hatred (3) Wang Tianhen

The earth was controlled even more closely by darkness and terror, and his heart was naturally even more flustered. But unexpectedly, after crawling for half an hour, he calmed down and carefully discerned, only to cry out in pain. It turned out that the direction he was walking was gradually opposite to the direction of his residence. When he calmed down and carefully discerned, he realized that he was getting farther and farther away from his residence. Anxious, he couldn't help but shed two lines of hot tears. If he wanted to turn back, his body was exhausted, and there was great danger. How could he take the risk and sacrifice himself in a muddle? But his old mother and young son were at home. How could he not risk going back? At this time, he was in a dilemma. He sat on the ground and cried for a while. Thinking that his old mother and young son might die, he couldn't help but cry bitterly!

But crying was useless. He realized this, decided to disregard the danger, tried his best to endure the pain, and still tried to find his way back. Unexpectedly, after crawling for a long time, he was finally blocked by stray bullets; and he also went the wrong way, and finally couldn't crawl home; and the sky finally brightened.

After dawn, the surrounding scenery could be seen clearly. It was truly miserable! Countless flustered refugees, just like himself in the night, were running in different directions, some running east and some running west. The sound of gunfire was still crackling, and the sound of planes was more frequent and louder than at night. The roar was endless, and the buildings in all directions were constantly emitting thick smoke and catching fire, reflecting the sky into a large red area. The thick smoke was like fog, covering the earth. He and countless refugees seemed to be facing the end of the world, not knowing where to die! At this time, he was extremely exhausted, as if he had become paralyzed. He looked at his former residence from afar, which was still very far away! But he also saw from afar that the location of his former residence was also ablaze with fire. The flames seemed to be burning his house, his heart, and the pain in his heart was more intense than the pain of his skin being broken and bleeding on his hands and face!

His former residence could only be viewed from afar and could not be reached! He had endured the pain and crawled all night. He couldn't stand up. He was indeed like a paralysis, unconsciously lying on the side of the road. Countless refugees passed by him, one by one as if they didn't see him, only caring about escaping for their lives. After a long time, he finally heard someone calling anxiously and panickedly in his ears: "Zhenzhong!" 丨his courtesy name丨 "Dad!" Calling like this. He opened his eyes and saw three people beside him. He couldn't help but jump up and say: "Am I in a dream?"

"Why are you here?" His brother-in-law Tai Qinjiang said.

"I thought you were already... why are you sleeping here?" His mother said with tears in her eyes.

"Dad! Why is your face covered in blood and dirt! Dad!" His young son Xiong'er also said with tears.

"Am I not dreaming!" He stared at them. Said again. "Is it really not a dream?"

"Zhenzhong! Why do you say it's a dream? Thanks to Qinjiang, he took us out and escaped, hiding east and west, suffering all night! Why did you disappear? When did you come out? I thought you had already met with misfortune. I didn't expect to meet you here. This is really God protecting us in the dark!" said the mother.

Local Supplement

Commentary

A Disguised Request for Romance

— A Warning to Fools

Recently, a classified advertisement in this newspaper's employment section, titled "Hiring Art Teacher," stated:

"A certain gentleman, a university professor, has ample free time in the afternoon and intends to study makeup, walking, and painting to cultivate his temperament. He is specifically seeking a young female art teacher for 20 hours per month, after lunch, with a monthly stipend of 20 to 30 yuan."

It is indeed true that art can cultivate one's temperament. After lunch, during the professor's free time, engaging in painting studies is quite appropriate. Serving in Shanghai, after completing one's inherent work, living alone feels uninteresting, and traveling around is wasteful. Learning to paint is the best way to restrain the mind and body while also pleasing one's temperament.

However, the teacher's qualifications are too strict. In my opinion, anyone who is an artist with painting experience is suitable, regardless of gender, age, male or female, old or young. Why insist on only seeking women, and only young women? Do young women possess more artistic talent and skill, and is their teaching method particularly superior and different from others? However, the gentleman is only in the initial stages of learning, so he does not need such an outstanding teacher. Anyone with a little knowledge of painting can serve as an instructor. In the ten miles of the foreign field, there are countless people who understand painting and can wield a few strokes. Advertisements appear in the morning, and responses arrive in the evening. Why insist on young women as a condition, abandoning the easy and pursuing the difficult?

Furthermore, there are many ways to cultivate one's temperament, such as music, chess, poetry, and calligraphy. All can be learned, and all can cultivate one's temperament. Is it only painting that has the possibility of cultivating one's temperament? Now, for the sake of cultivating his temperament, he must learn to paint, and to learn to paint, he must have a young woman as a tutor. Does the cultivation of temperament through painting become twice as effective once taught by a young woman? However, there is no such reason.

Therefore, I am thinking for the gentleman. If he is committed to painting in order to cultivate his temperament and is seeking a teacher, then this advertisement is almost equal to zero. Truly talented and skilled young women in art will not covet the meager monthly salary of 20 to 30 yuan to demean themselves and condescend to teach. On the other hand, those who are willing to gracefully condescend and apply are those who have no real knowledge. This reason is very clear. If so, then the recruiter will still find it difficult to fulfill his desire for learning. If the drunkard's intention is not in the wine, but simply wants to use the recruitment of a teacher as a name to conduct a romantic experiment, then it is better to be straightforward and write "Seeking Girlfriend," "Seeking Lover," "Seeking..." etc., which would be much more straightforward.

Popular Literature & Art

Poem on the Death of Battalion Commander Luo

— Mengshao'an Wangzhu

Battalion Commander Luo Kun of the First Battalion of the 78th Division died in the Xiaochangmiao battle on March 1st. In this battle, the Japanese soldiers attacked our battalion's position with all their might. The battalion commander fought to the death, killing 700 enemies. The news reached us more than a month later. This poem is to mourn him.

The battlefield is silent during the day, the sky is ashen,

Stubborn clouds press down on the formation, the formation does not open.

Thousands of butterflies suddenly fly out, (Butterfly soldiers are Japanese bandits, see the History of Ming)

The sound of killing is like the sea,排空而来,

Fire and lightning explode from the nine heavens and nine earths,

The lone army resists the wall,危一髮,

The public anger makes a sound,万鬼瘖,

Fights to kill the bandits first,

The bandits see the public come,疑飞神,

All the puppets are on the ground,

Our army is like a dragon, the enemy is like grass,

The big call 陷阵山 for 倒,

Till morning till noon, the war does not 疲,

The enemy army of 700 are all meat 糜,

The public force is not exhausted, the gun suddenly breaks,

In his hand, there are still a few bullets,

Wrapped in sores and fighting again, the armor is all red,

This heart and blood are all melted into iron,

貫日雄虹万丈起,

汉家虎将终战死,

That night, our army's drums did not Yang,

The whole army retreats thirty 里,

It is a pity that the crowd is too different,

Otherwise, who can pull the five peaks,

The battlefield after the 劫者愁,

莽苍不可收,

I do not know what is the public bone,

The sky is阴雨湿魂咿嘠,

安得起公　　貅,

往集餘燼剪我仇,

侧身西望徒繁忧,

Feelings on Reading Poems from Haizanglou

— Mengshao'an Wang

The Bronze Di was stroked for twenty years,

With a wave of his hand, he turned Jianghai into Du Fanchuan.

The world in between the lines has changed,

Still, he bows to the cuckoo in the empty forest.

White hair and a cane bed, he hasn't returned at night,

Tears fill the Qin court, the old minister's clothes.

The breeze and moon over Wushan are unharmed,

Tell the western crows not to fly at night.
