Assassinate Ma Zhanshan

— Chen Zhuzun

Reports state that Ma Zhanshan is a minister in the puppet Manchukuo government. The people of the country are saddened by Ma Zhanshan's lack of a good end and resent Zhang Xueliang's inaction. Therefore, this poem is composed. March Yesterday, a loyal minister is today a traitor. Although the tombs are lonely, the Han Dynasty betrayed virtue. A person's honor and disgrace are not worth discussing. When the節 has fallen, it is a pity. The waters under Heilongjiang are 潺湲, as if sighing deeply for the general.

Encourage General Ma Zhanshan

— Chen Zhuzun

Today's report states that General Ma Zhanshan has sent a telegram continuing to resist the Japanese. The people of the country commend him for this. This poem is composed on April 14th.

Last year, I wrote a poem praising the general,

The other day, I wrote a poem condemning the general.

Today, I write a poem encouraging the general.

Alas, may General Ma be encouraged!

Since the barbarians have come to the three provinces,

The main generals have heard of non-resistance.

The people of the country despise them like pigs.

The great humiliation of the world falls on them.

Only you, sir, shook your arm on the Black River,

And fought bloodily for months, performing wonders.

The people's songs soar to the sky,

榆粟捐财何缤纷,

英名赫赫中天县,

家家买丝绣平原,

铜像峥嵘遍城邨,

香烟聲名尤赫喧,

Independent support is difficult to support a large building.

The entire army re-formed and returned to Hailun.

Being loyal to the Han and following one's heart is the best.

It's a pity that Puyi is昏復昏,

Willing to turn Manchuria into Korea.

When you occasionally entered and exited the puppet country's gates,

People scolded you for raising the banner of surrender.

Although I doubted you, I could not argue.

Three men speaking in the market say there are crouching tigers.

Writing a poem to刺君 is still doubtful of injustice.

One should leave righteousness to the universe.

Now I have read your declaration,

Truly, your heart is forgivable.

The sun and moon pass through the heavens, and things come to swallow them.

In a moment, the light will illuminate all directions.

世人宁得轻輊轩,

I hope you will work hard to restore national sovereignty.

大复国仇报国恩,

Riches and honor are floating clouds, what is enough to say?

Only loyalty and righteousness are the nation's soul,

Protecting it will strengthen the country, and losing it will ruin it.

I have the Spring and Autumn annals in my poetic pen,

And I will write in large letters the five generals of the Republic of China:

Ma Zhanshan, Cai Tingkai, Jiang Guangnai, Tan Qixiu, and Weng Zhaoyuan.

Public Science

Continued Smoke Screen Shells

— Yun Juan

Smoke screen shells can not only provide concealment to avoid enemy attacks, but also can be used to assist in military operations, such as: ambushes, troop movements, and replacing military orders. Because soldiers are lying in trenches, it is sometimes difficult to issue orders effectively. Using the color of smoke to represent military orders is more effective. It can also make the enemy believe it is poison gas, forcing them to wear masks, thereby reducing the enemy's combat capability. (During the European war, smoke screen shells were often used in conjunction with poison gas to make it impossible for the enemy to identify which type of poison gas it was.)

Tetrachlorotin (SnCl4) is the most common of these, and a manufacturing method was previously described by Li Jun in this publication. However, there is a simpler method than the one described by Li Jun: (1) It can be made from stannous chloride (SnCl2) plus aqua regia. This method is widely used commercially; it forms crystals, known as strong tin. (2) A small piece of tin, add a small amount of hydrochloric acid (if it is too slow, it can be heated slightly). Separately, add two cubic centimeters of ferric chloride to five cubic centimeters of water. Then, add the above tin solution drop by drop until a color change occurs, and a white, thick smoke will be obtained. The chemical formula is as follows:

2FeCl3 SnCl2 2FeCl2 SnCl4

Ferric chloride Stannous chloride Ferrous chloride Tetrachlorotin

In addition to being used for smoke screens, tetrachlorotin is often used as a mordant. Therefore, it is also very important in the dyeing industry.

Casual Talk

Miss and Old Maid

— Wu

Because the spring breeze has blown away the war clouds over Shanghai and bestowed infinite warmth on the noble citizens, Miss Li, as usual, led her own old maid (a potential nanny) back lazily from the park.

At the corner of a road, several fundraising teams were standing in front of a small cigarette and paper shop, as could be seen from the flags. One of the young women was pleading to the people in this way: "We have all been fired by the Japanese textile mill. If we don't work for a day, we don't eat for a day. We ourselves can sometimes endure being hungry, but the children at home cry all day long, which is truly heartbreaking... Please donate a little to do a good deed and save lives!"

This kind of tearful crying, in the eyes of our noble Miss Li, was truly ridiculous; first of all, they are workers, and what does it matter if a worker temporarily has no food to eat because of national affairs? ... So she just sneered and left them. Of course, the fundraisers could only "save their breath" to her.

Not far away, she discovered that her old maid was panting and chasing after her from a distance. This was simply worth her throwing a tantrum.

"Why do you always like to get involved with them? You low-life!" "No, they are too pitiful. I donated all my two yuan wages to them."

"Damn thing!" A palm print was left on the old maid's face. "You have so much spare money? I'll make sure they don't give you a single penny in the future!"

But the old maid firmly believed: she herself had worked as a worker, so only she understood the suffering of the workers. The young lady was the daughter of a large family, she would never know and would never want to know their lives. So, this is the difference between "Miss" and "Old Maid".

From East to West

Saving the Nation Through Food

— Chen Jiyun

Since the market opened on April 1st, all sectors and industries have expressed their patriotism, all claiming to "endure pain and resist for the long term." In reality, they are all profiting from the name of national crisis! The day before yesterday, I went out on business and sat quietly in the tram. I suddenly found a calendar on my body. Taking it out to look at it, I realized it was an advertisement for XXX, a promotional item using a calendar. The calendar had the four characters "Saving the Nation Through Food" written on it. After reading it, I felt that this merchant was very enthusiastic about saving the nation. Our people should be twelve thousand times grateful.

We know that if it is called food, it must certainly be able to fill the stomach. However, this kind of food (seasonal fruits, weekly delicacies...) is not essential, and is entirely extra food for the rich, which can be said to be eaten for fun.

In this time of national crisis, everything must embrace a tight policy. As for food, it is best to adopt a one-dish system, save some money, and purchase some defensive items. Purchase practical and effective military supplies for the country. It is found that what our country is currently most threatened by are warships, cannons, and aircraft. Defending against enemy aircraft dropping bombs is the most urgent task at present. In view of the traces of devastation left by Japanese aircraft rampant in Zhabei, Jiangwan, Wusong, and other places, for the sake of self-defense and national defense, regardless of whether this meeting is successful or not, we should quickly raise funds and engage in air defense facilities. In the event of an emergency, in addition to the national defense of the positions, all households and shops can be spared from the trampling of enemy aircraft, which is better than unnecessary food in the stomach. Therefore, this kind of food is enough to destroy the country.

Zhou Yu is appointed as the special agent for the defendants An Jixiang and Zhang Guogui. The defendants are ordered to appear in court on time for argument without delay. This public notice is hereby served. The above is for the information of the defendants An Jixiang and Zhang Guogui.

▲Judgment on the divorce case of Li Peiqiu versus Lü Dingyi (Main Text): The marital relationship between the plaintiff and the defendant shall be dissolved. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. The above is for the information of the defendant Lü Dingyi.

Civil Judgment:

Du Bifu et al. versus Zhao Zhu shi, rent arrears case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The second-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellants themselves.

Gu Xiguang versus Zhang Songtao, eviction appeal case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The second-instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲Yi Shun Long hao versus Wu Jinsheng, debt case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff a mortgage loan of 230 yuan in silver currency. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Xu Xiaochao versus Ding Shaoheng, house rental case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff rent arrears of 160 yuan in foreign currency and shall vacate the house. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Civil Rulings:

Shan Jiping's application for detention and assurance to pursue payment: The court is informed of the statement. A summons shall be issued for strict pursuit of the case. This ruling.

▲Zhu Qinsheng's application for strict pursuit of the guarantor for execution: The court is informed of the statement. The debtor shall still be summoned to court for execution. The request to summon and pursue the guarantor is not approved because there is no such execution title in the file. This ruling.

▲Yang Buyun's application for execution against the property of the principal debtor: The court is informed of the statement. The court shall still follow the summons to the court for interrogation. This ruling.

▲Gu Jingqing's application for execution: The court is informed of the statement. The court shall await further summons and interrogation. This ruling.

▲Ge Taojuan's application to collect payment: The court is informed of the statement. The applicant shall come to the court at 9:00 AM on the 26th of this month to collect the payment. This ruling.

▲Cai Wenqing's application for execution: The court is informed of the statement. The court shall await the issuance of a summons for interrogation and pursuit. This ruling.

▲Li Qianwan's application for reopening of arguments due to a debt dispute: The court is informed of the statement. The case has already been argued to conclusion. The application for reopening of arguments shall not be considered. This ruling.

▲Li Qianwan's application for authorization of an agent due to a debt dispute: The court is informed of the statement. The case has already been argued to conclusion. The parties shall be informed immediately. This ruling.

▲Chen Fengshi's application for recordation due to loss of a contract and seal: The court is informed of the statement. It is stated that remedies should be sought for the loss of the passbook, contract, and seal. Applying for recordation with the court is practically useless and insufficient to provide a basis. The proposed report is not described in detail and is particularly inaccurate. The application is difficult to approve. This ruling.

▲Yang Han shi's application for recordation of adopting a son-in-law for her daughter-in-law: The court is informed of the statement. According to the absolute freedom of marriage for men and women, the agent should be responsible for the matter. Since the daughter-in-law has already willingly adopted a son-in-law, there is no danger to speak of, and there is no need for recordation. The parties shall be informed immediately. This ruling. (The above is dated April 21st)
